    function toggleFooterSection(button) {
  var content = button.parentNode.nextElementSibling;
  if (content.style.display === "none") {
    content.style.display = "block";
    button.textContent = "-";
  } else {
    content.style.display = "none";
    button.textContent = "+";
  }
}

</script>

<script>
(function() {
  var debounceTimer = null;
  var activeIndex = -1;
  var currentResults = [];
  var currentQuery = '';
  var openDropdown = null;
  var currentInput = null;
  var isDesktop = window.innerWidth >= 1024;
  window.addEventListener('resize', function() { isDesktop = window.innerWidth >= 1024; });

  // Single dropdown appended to body — never inside the form
  var dd = document.createElement('div');
  dd.className = 'ds-dropdown';
  document.body.appendChild(dd);

  function positionDropdown(input) {
    var rect = input.getBoundingClientRect();
    if (isDesktop) {
      // Align right edge of dropdown to right edge of input, below input
      dd.style.top = (rect.bottom + 8) + 'px';
      dd.style.left = '';
      dd.style.right = '';
      // Render first, then measure to right-align
      dd.style.left = '0px';
      var ddW = dd.offsetWidth;
      var inputRight = rect.right;
      var leftPos = inputRight - ddW;
      if (leftPos < 8) leftPos = 8; // don't overflow left edge
      dd.style.left = leftPos + 'px';
    } else {
      // Mobile: full width below navbar
      dd.style.top = '60px';
      dd.style.left = '8px';
      dd.style.right = '8px';
    }
  }

  function renderLoading() {
    var html = '<div class="ds-loading">';
    var count = isDesktop ? 6 : 3;
    for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {
      if (isDesktop) {
        html += '<div class="ds-skeleton"><div class="ds-skeleton-poster"></div><div class="ds-skeleton-line"></div><div class="ds-skeleton-line"></div></div>';
      } else {
        html += '<div class="ds-skeleton"><div class="ds-skeleton-poster"></div><div class="ds-skeleton-lines"><div class="ds-skeleton-line"></div><div class="ds-skeleton-line"></div></div></div>';
      }
    }
    html += '</div>';
    dd.innerHTML = html;
    dd.classList.add('ds-visible');
    if (currentInput) positionDropdown(currentInput);
    openDropdown = dd;
  }

  function renderResults(items, query) {
    if (!items.length) {
      dd.innerHTML = '<div class="ds-empty">\u10E8\u10D4\u10D3\u10D4\u10D2\u10D4\u10D1\u10D8 \u10D5\u10D4\u10E0 \u10DB\u10DD\u10D8\u10EB\u10D4\u10D1\u10DC\u10D0</div>';
      dd.classList.add('ds-visible');
      if (currentInput) positionDropdown(currentInput);
      openDropdown = dd;
      return;
    }
    var searchUrl = '/?do=search&subaction=search&titleonly=3&story=' + encodeURIComponent(query);
    var html = '<div class="ds-grid">';
    for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
      var item = items[i];
      var posterSrc = item.poster || '/templates/adjaratest-2/images/poster-dark.svg';
      var displayTitle = item.title;
      var sepIdx = displayTitle.indexOf(' / ');
      if (sepIdx === -1) sepIdx = displayTitle.indexOf(' | ');
      if (sepIdx > 0) displayTitle = displayTitle.substring(0, sepIdx);

      html += '<a href="' + item.url + '" class="ds-item" data-index="' + i + '">';
      html += '<img class="ds-item-poster" src="' + posterSrc + '" alt="" loading="lazy" onerror="this.src=\'/templates/adjaratest-2/images/poster-dark.svg\'">';
      html += '<div class="ds-item-title">' + escapeHtml(displayTitle) + '</div>';
      html += '</a>';
    }
    html += '</div>';
    html += '<a href="' + searchUrl + '" class="ds-viewall">\u10E7\u10D5\u10D4\u10DA\u10D0 \u10E8\u10D4\u10D3\u10D4\u10D2\u10D8\u10E1 \u10DC\u10D0\u10EE\u10D5\u10D0 \u2192</a>';
    dd.innerHTML = html;
    dd.classList.add('ds-visible');
    if (currentInput) positionDropdown(currentInput);
    openDropdown = dd;
    activeIndex = -1;
    currentResults = items;
  }

  function closeDropdown() {
    dd.classList.remove('ds-visible');
    openDropdown = null;
    activeIndex = -1;
    currentResults = [];
  }

  function escapeHtml(str) {
    var el = document.createElement('div');
    el.textContent = str;
    return el.innerHTML;
  }

  function updateActive() {
    var items = dd.querySelectorAll('.ds-item');
    for (var i = 0; i < items.length; i++) {
      items[i].classList.toggle('ds-active', i === activeIndex);
    }
    if (activeIndex >= 0 && items[activeIndex]) {
      items[activeIndex].scrollIntoView({ block: 'nearest', inline: 'nearest' });
    }
  }

  function doSearch(input) {
    var q = input.value.trim();
    currentQuery = q;
    currentInput = input;
    if (q.length < 2) {
      closeDropdown();
      return;
    }
    renderLoading();

    fetch('/api_search.php?q=' + encodeURIComponent(q))
      .then(function(r) { return r.json(); })
      .then(function(data) {
        if (input.value.trim() !== currentQuery) return;
        renderResults(data, q);
      })
      .catch(function() {
        dd.innerHTML = '<div class="ds-empty">\u10E8\u10D4\u10EA\u10D3\u10DD\u10DB\u10D8\u10E1\u10D0\u10E1 \u10DB\u10DD\u10EE\u10D3\u10D0 \u10E8\u10D4\u10EA\u10D3\u10DD\u10DB\u10D0</div>';
      });
  }

  function initInput(input) {
    input.addEventListener('input', function() {
      clearTimeout(debounceTimer);
      var self = this;
      debounceTimer = setTimeout(function() {
        doSearch(self);
      }, 300);
    });

    input.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      if (!openDropdown) return;
      var items = dd.querySelectorAll('.ds-item');
      if (!items.length) return;

      var next = (e.key === 'ArrowRight' && isDesktop) || e.key === 'ArrowDown';
      var prev = (e.key === 'ArrowLeft' && isDesktop) || e.key === 'ArrowUp';

      if (next) {
        e.preventDefault();
        activeIndex = Math.min(activeIndex + 1, items.length - 1);
        updateActive();
      } else if (prev) {
        e.preventDefault();
        activeIndex = Math.max(activeIndex - 1, -1);
        updateActive();
      } else if (e.key === 'Enter' && activeIndex >= 0) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var href = items[activeIndex].getAttribute('href');
        if (href) window.location.href = href;
      } else if (e.key === 'Escape') {
        e.preventDefault();
        closeDropdown();
      }
    });

    input.addEventListener('focus', function() {
      if (this.value.trim().length >= 2) {
        doSearch(this);
      }
    });
  }

  var inputs = document.querySelectorAll('input[name="story"]');
  for (var i = 0; i < inputs.length; i++) {
    initInput(inputs[i]);
  }

  document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    if (openDropdown && !e.target.closest('.ds-dropdown') && e.target.name !== 'story') {
      closeDropdown();
    }
  });

  window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
    if (openDropdown && currentInput) positionDropdown(currentInput);
  }, { passive: true });
})();
</script>
<!-- Dropdown Search / დასასრული -->
